In contrast, concentrated solvated metal atoms lead to supported nanoclusters with larger size distributions and diameters, rendering them ineffective. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Despite the desirable exothermic nature and the limited coke formation, ODH based on oxygen is confronted with the challenge of over oxidation of alkane to CO and CO2, as well as the possibility of reaction runaway.\"\n          [2] \"On the other hand, a N2O/O2 oxidant mixture could enhance the propylene selectivity by 25% for the vanadia-catalyzed propane ODH reactions, but this increased selectivity could be obtained only at low propane conversion (110%).\"\n          [3] \"Some studies have also been performed on the effect of H2S or other sulfur species on the ODH reactions of light alkanes.\"\n          [4] \"Therefore, the present work aims at acquiring a better understanding of the effect of H2S in the alkane ODH reaction.\"", "English": "Analyzing the use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP), it appears that N2O can enhance propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. Specifically, a N2O/O2 mixture was found to increase propylene selectivity by 25% for the vanadia-catalyzed propane ODH reactions, but this improvement was only possible at low propane conversion levels (110%). This suggests that N2O can be advantageous in enhancing propylene selectivity, but the operational conditions might limit its practical application. Challenges associated with catalyst deactivation and stability in the ODHP process are critical issues. Catalysts employed in this process include vanadia and mixed-metal oxides, which are known for their high thermal stability, large surface areas, and favorable reducibility and basicity that promote ODH activity and selectivity. However, these systems have not yet shown product yields comparable to those obtained by current industrial technologies for olefin production. Strategies to address these limitations could involve improving catalyst design to enhance stability and deactivation resistance, optimizing operating conditions to maximize selectivity without compromising conversion, and exploring novel oxidants or additives that can further enhance propylene selectivity without increasing the risk of overoxidation or reaction runaway. Research directions might include studying the synergistic effects of different oxidants in combination with specific catalysts, investigating the role of sulfur species in dictating product selectivity in alkane ODH reactions, and developing advanced catalysts with improved selectivity and stability for practical implementation of N2O-ODHP.", "Chinese": "在氧化脱氢化丙烷（ODHP）过程中使用二氧化氮（N2O）作为氧化剂，分析显示N2O可以提高丙烯选择性，与其它氧化剂相比具有优势。具体而言，N2O/O2混合物被发现可以将用范迪催化剂催化丙烷ODHP反应时的丙烯选择性提高25%，但这种选择性的提升仅能在较低的丙烷转化率（110%）下实现。这表明N2O可能在增强丙烯选择性方面有利，但其操作条件可能会限制其实用性。与ODHP过程相关的催化剂失活和稳定性问题是一些关键挑战。所使用的催化剂包括范迪和混合金属氧化物，这些物质以其高热稳定性、大表面积、有利于脱氢活性和选择性的还原性和碱性而著称。然而，这些系统尚未显示出与当前工业技术用于生产烯烃的产量相当的产品。为应对这些局限性，可以采取的策略包括改进催化剂设计以增强稳定性和防止失活，优化操作条件以最大化选择性而不牺牲转化率，并探索不同氧化剂的新型组合或添加剂以进一步提高丙烯选择性，同时降低过氧化或反应失控的风险。研究方向可能包括研究不同氧化剂与特定催化剂的协同作用效果，探究硫物种在烷烃ODHP反应中决定产物选择性的作用，以及开发具有改进选择性和稳定性的新型催化剂以实现N2O-ODHP的实用实施。", "Doi": "10.1021/jp410750c"},

{"Quotes": "[1] \"N2O induces the reduction of Mo at the surface of the catalyst. This is supposed to occur through an inhibition of the adsorption of O2 because of the presence of N2O at the surface of the catalyst, which thus slows down the reoxidation rate of the catalyst.\"\n          [2] \"N2O promotes the decrease in the oxidation rate of the catalysts, so promoting its reduction.\"\n          [3] \"Higher is the concentration of N2O, higher is the degree of reduction of catalysts.\"\n          [4] \"The addition of N2O in a feed formed of propane and molecular oxygen could have important implications in the catalytic performances of the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane into propylene on nickel molybdate catalysts.\"\n          [5] \"N2O needs the presence of molecular oxygen to produce propylene durably.\"\n          [6] \"N2O promotes the decrease in the oxidation rate of the catalysts, so promoting its reduction.\"\n          [7] \"Some ppm of N2O only lead to a slight reduction of the catalyst, and bring about a decrease of the conversion of propane, increases of the yield and selectivity in propylene, a decrease of the formation of CO2 and of the oxygen consumption.\"\n          [8] \"When the amount of N2O increases, the reduction of the catalyst is deeper.\"\n          [9] \"Propylene is produced from propane in presence of pure N2O. But this probably occurs only under transitory conditions as N2O probably needs the presence of molecular oxygen to produce propylene durably.\"", "English": "Nitrous oxide (N2O) can be used as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP), which helps to reduce the rate of oxidation of the catalysts, thereby promoting their reduction. The degree of reduction increases with the concentration of N2O. The use of N2O in ODHP can have significant implications for improving propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. However, N2O requires the presence of molecular oxygen to produce propylene durably. When the amount of N2O increases, the reduction of the catalyst becomes deeper, leading to a decrease in the conversion of propane, an increase in the yield and selectivity in propylene, a decrease in the formation of CO2, and a reduction in oxygen consumption. In certain conditions, propylene can be produced from propane in the presence of pure N2O, but this likely occurs only temporarily since N2O needs the presence of molecular oxygen to produce propylene consistently.", "Chinese": "在丙烷氧化脱氢（ODHP）过程中，可以使用氮氧化物（N2O）作为氧化剂，它有助于降低催化剂的氧化速率，从而促进其还原。N2O浓度越高，催化剂的还原程度越高。在ODHP中使用N2O可以显著提高丙烯选择性，与其它氧化剂相比。然而，N2O需要分子氧的存在才能持久地产生丙烯。当N2O的量增加时，催化剂的还原程度更深，导致丙烷转化率下降，丙烯产率和选择性增加，CO2形成减少，氧消耗降低。在某些条件下，纯N2O可以诱导丙烷转化为丙烯，但这很可能只是暂时现象，因为N2O需要分子氧的存在才能持续产生丙烯。", "Doi": "10.1016/S0926-860X(03)00103-0"},
{"Quotes": "[1] \"Although hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) has recently been identified as a highly efficient catalyst for the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) reaction, the reaction mechanisms, especially regarding radical chemistry of this system, remain elusive.\"\n          [2] \"Now, the first direct experimental evidence of gas-phase methyl radicals (CH3.) in the ODHP reaction over boron-based catalysts is achieved by using online synchrotron vacuum ultraviolet photoionization mass spectroscopy (SVUV-PIMS), which uncovers the existence of gas-phase radical pathways.\"\n          [3] \"Combined with density functional theory (DFT) calculations, the results demonstrate that propene is mainly generated on the catalyst surface from the CH activation of propane, while C2 and C1 products can be formed via both surface-mediated and gas-phase pathways.\"\n          [4] \"The high thermodynamic (and kinetic) unfavorability of the subsequent CH activation by the BOB oxygen is explained by poor redox ability of the surface, which differs from conventional ODHP catalysts such as vanadia and other transition-metal oxides.\"\n          [5] \"In the absence of an oxidant such as O2, the C3H7 intermediate is inert to surface-mediated CH activation and further oxidation (Supporting Information, FigureS32), though gas-phase unimolecular cleavage could still occur.\"\n          [6] \"Our findings provide new insights towards understanding the ODHP reaction mechanisms and pathways over boron-based catalysts and are of significance for developing highly selective catalysts for alkane ODH.\"", "English": "The use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) process offers several advantages, particularly in terms of propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. Recent studies have identified hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) as a highly efficient catalyst for ODHP, although the detailed reaction mechanisms, especially those involving radical chemistry, remain unclear. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Steam-activated Fe-zeolites are highly active and selective catalysts for the ODH of propane with N2O, achieving propylene yields up to 25% at 723 K and space velocities of 400,000 ml h1 g1 cat.\"\n          [2] \"The presence of extraframework iron species, generated during steam treatment, is essential for producing active catalysts.\"\n          [3] \"FeZSM-5 shows a remarkable resistance against deactivation, while a very rapid and complete deactivation occurred in FeBEA.\"\n          [4] \"The initial propene yield over FeZSM-5 and FeBEA was remarkably higher than over commercial H-ZSM-5 and H-BEA (with 3040 times lower iron content), although the residual activities after 400 min on stream were very similar.\"\n          [5] \"The interaction of C3H8 with the iron zeolites in the absence of N2O did not lead to propene production, indicating the essential role of the oxidant for propane dehydrogenation.\"\n          [6] \"Steam activation is essential to achieve superior catalytic performances.\"\n          [7] \"The essential role of iron in the reaction can be clearly concluded from the significantly higher C3H8 and N2O conversions over ex-FeZSM-5 and ex-FeBEA, as compared to ex-H-ZSM-5 and ex-H-BEA.\"\n          [8] \"In general terms, the coking rate in zeolites depends on the acidic sites (number and strength), the zeolite structure, and the reaction conditions.\"\n          [9] \"The higher deactivation resistance of steam-activated ex-FeZSM-5 in ODHP with N2O is unclear at this stage, but can be tentatively related to the different iron constitutions in both catalysts and/or the different porous structure associated to the presence of aluminum in the original zeolite framework.\"", "English": "Nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) provides advantages in terms of propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants, thanks to its ability to selectively donate oxygen atoms. High-performance catalysts such as FeZSM-5 and FeBEA are used, achieving propylene yields up to 25% at 723 K and operating under high space velocities of 400,000 ml h1 g1 cat. A significant challenge is the catalyst deactivation due to coke formation, although it can be mitigated through regeneration in oxygen at 773 K. The role of iron is critical, with steam-activated Fe-zeolites demonstrating remarkable resistance against deactivation, contrasting with the rapid and complete deactivation seen in FeBEA. The initial propene yield over FeZSM-5 and FeBEA is notably higher than over commercial H-ZSM-5 and H-BEA (with 3040 times less iron content), yet residual activities after 400 minutes of operation are similar. {"Quotes": "[1] \"N2O induces the reduction of Mo at the surface of the catalyst. The degree of reduction increases with the concentration of N2O. The use of N2O in ODHP can have significant implications for improving propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Although hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) has recently been identified as a highly efficient catalyst for the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) reaction, the reaction mechanisms, especially regarding radical chemistry of this system, remain elusive.\"\n          [2] \"Now, the first direct experimental evidence of gas-phase methyl radicals (CH3.) in the ODHP reaction over boron-based catalysts is achieved by using online synchrotron vacuum ultraviolet photoionization mass spectroscopy (SVUV-PIMS), which uncovers the existence of gas-phase radical pathways.\"\n          [3] \"Combined with density functional theory (DFT) calculations, the results demonstrate that propene is mainly generated on the catalyst surface from the CH activation of propane, while C2 and C1 products can be formed via both surface-mediated and gas-phase pathways.\"\n          [4] \"The high thermodynamic (and kinetic) unfavorability of the subsequent CH activation by the BOB oxygen is explained by poor redox ability of the surface, which differs from conventional ODHP catalysts such as vanadia and other transition-metal oxides.\"\n          [5] \"In the absence of an oxidant such as O2, the C3H7 intermediate is inert to surface-mediated CH activation and further oxidation (Supporting Information, FigureS32), though gas-phase unimolecular cleavage could still occur.\"\n          [6] \"Our findings provide new insights towards understanding the ODHP reaction mechanisms and pathways over boron-based catalysts and are of significance for developing highly selective catalysts for alkane ODH.\"", "English": "The use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) process offers several advantages, particularly in terms of propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. Recent studies have identified hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) as a highly efficient catalyst for ODHP, although the detailed reaction mechanisms, especially those involving radical chemistry, remain unclear. The discovery of gas-phase methyl radicals (CH3.) in the ODHP reaction over boron-based catalysts, confirmed by online synchrotron vacuum ultraviolet photoionization mass spectroscopy (SVUV-PIMS), provides new insights into the existence of gas-phase radical pathways in this process.\n\n          The results from density functional theory (DFT) calculations show that propene is primarily generated on the catalyst surface from the activation of propane's CH bonds, with products of C2 and C1 forming through both surface-mediated and gas-phase pathways. {"Quotes": "[1] \"N2O induces the reduction of Mo at the surface of the catalyst. This is supposed to occur through an inhibition of the adsorption of O2 because of the presence of N2O at the surface of the catalyst, which thus slows down the reoxidation rate of the catalyst.\"\n          [2] \"N2O promotes the decrease in the oxidation rate of the catalysts, so promoting its reduction.\"\n          [3] \"Higher is the concentration of N2O, higher is the degree of reduction of catalysts.\"\n          [4] \"The addition of N2O in a feed formed of propane and molecular oxygen could have important implications in the catalytic performances of the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane into propylene on nickel molybdate catalysts.\"\n          [5] \"N2O needs the presence of molecular oxygen to produce propylene durably.\"\n          [6] \"N2O promotes the decrease in the oxidation rate of the catalysts, so promoting its reduction.\"\n          [7] \"Some ppm of N2O only lead to a slight reduction of the catalyst, and bring about a decrease of the conversion of propane, increases of the yield and selectivity in propylene, a decrease of the formation of CO2 and of the oxygen consumption.\"\n          [8] \"When the amount of N2O increases, the reduction of the catalyst is deeper.\"\n          [9] \"Propylene is produced from propane in presence of pure N2O. But this probably occurs only under transitory conditions as N2O probably needs the presence of molecular oxygen to produce propylene durably.\"", "English": "Nitrous oxide (N2O) can be used as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP), which helps to reduce the rate of oxidation of the catalysts, thereby promoting their reduction. The degree of reduction increases with the concentration of N2O. The use of N2O in ODHP can have significant implications for improving propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. However, N2O requires the presence of molecular oxygen to produce propylene durably. When the amount of N2O increases, the reduction of the catalyst becomes deeper, leading to a decrease in the conversion of propane, an increase in the yield and selectivity in propylene, a decrease in the formation of CO2, and a reduction in oxygen consumption. In certain conditions, propylene can be produced from propane in the presence of pure N2O, but this likely occurs only temporarily since N2O needs the presence of molecular oxygen to produce propylene consistently.", "Chinese": "在丙烷氧化脱氢（ODHP）过程中，可以使用氮氧化物（N2O）作为氧化剂，它有助于降低催化剂的氧化速率，从而促进其还原。N2O浓度越高，催化剂的还原程度越高。在ODHP中使用N2O可以显著提高丙烯选择性，与其它氧化剂相比。然而，N2O需要分子氧的存在才能持久地产生丙烯。当N2O的量增加时，催化剂的还原程度更深，导致丙烷转化率下降，丙烯产率和选择性增加，CO2形成减少，氧消耗降低。在某些条件下，纯N2O可以诱导丙烷转化为丙烯，但这很可能只是暂时现象，因为N2O需要分子氧的存在才能持续产生丙烯。", "Doi": "10.1016/S0926-860X(03)00103-0"},
{"Quotes": "[1] \"Although hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) has recently been identified as a highly efficient catalyst for the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) reaction, the reaction mechanisms, especially regarding radical chemistry of this system, remain elusive.\"\n          [2] \"Now, the first direct experimental evidence of gas-phase methyl radicals (CH3.) in the ODHP reaction over boron-based catalysts is achieved by using online synchrotron vacuum ultraviolet photoionization mass spectroscopy (SVUV-PIMS), which uncovers the existence of gas-phase radical pathways.\"\n          [3] \"Combined with density functional theory (DFT) calculations, the results demonstrate that propene is mainly generated on the catalyst surface from the CH activation of propane, while C2 and C1 products can be formed via both surface-mediated and gas-phase pathways.\"\n          [4] \"The high thermodynamic (and kinetic) unfavorability of the subsequent CH activation by the BOB oxygen is explained by poor redox ability of the surface, which differs from conventional ODHP catalysts such as vanadia and other transition-metal oxides.\"\n          [5] \"In the absence of an oxidant such as O2, the C3H7 intermediate is inert to surface-mediated CH activation and further oxidation (Supporting Information, FigureS32), though gas-phase unimolecular cleavage could still occur.\"\n          [6] \"Our findings provide new insights towards understanding the ODHP reaction mechanisms and pathways over boron-based catalysts and are of significance for developing highly selective catalysts for alkane ODH.\"", "English": "The use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) process offers several advantages, particularly in terms of propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. Recent studies have identified hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) as a highly efficient catalyst for ODHP, although the detailed reaction mechanisms, especially those involving radical chemistry, remain unclear. The discovery of gas-phase methyl radicals (CH3.) in the ODHP reaction over boron-based catalysts, confirmed by online synchrotron vacuum ultraviolet photoionization mass spectroscopy (SVUV-PIMS), provides new insights into the existence of gas-phase radical pathways in this process.\n\n          The results from density functional theory (DFT) calculations show that propene is primarily generated on the catalyst surface from the activation of propane's CH bonds, with products of C2 and C1 forming through both surface-mediated and gas-phase pathways. The high thermodynamic (and kinetic) inefficiency of subsequent CH activation by BOB oxygen is explained by the surface's poor redox ability, distinguishing it from conventional ODHP catalysts like vanadia and other transition-metal oxides. In the absence of an oxidant like O2, the C3H7 intermediate is relatively inert to surface-mediated CH activation and further oxidation, but gas-phase unimolecular cleavage can still occur.\n\n          These findings are significant for understanding the ODHP reaction mechanisms over boron-based catalysts and for developing highly selective catalysts for alkane oxidative dehydrogenation (ODH).", "Chinese": "使用氮氧化物（N2O）作为丙烷氧化脱氢（ODHP）过程中的氧化剂，尤其在丙烯选择性方面具有优势，与其它氧化剂相比。最近的研究已经确认六方硼氮化物（h-BN）是ODHP过程中的高效催化剂，尽管此过程的具体反应机制，特别是涉及到自由基化学的部分，仍然难以捉摸。在线同步辐射真空紫外光离子质谱法（SVUV-PIMS）证实了在硼基催化剂上进行ODHP反应时存在气相甲基自由基（CH3.），这一发现为理解该过程中存在的气相自由基途径提供了新见解。\n\n          密度泛函理论（DFT）计算的结果表明，丙烯主要在催化剂表面上从丙烷的CH键激活产生，C2和C1产品则通过表面介导和气相途径形成。随后由BOB氧引发的CH激活的高热力学（和动力学）不利性是由表面的弱氧化还原能力所解释的，这与传统ODHP催化剂如钒酸盐和其他过渡金属氧化物有别。在缺乏如O2这样的氧化剂时，C3H7中间体相对不易于表面介导的CH激活和进一步氧化，但气相单分子裂解仍可能发生。\n\n          这些发现对于理解硼基催化剂上的ODHP反应机制以及开发用于烷烃氧化脱氢（ODH）的高效选择性催化剂具有重要意义。", "Doi": "10.1002/anie.202002440"},
{"Quotes": "[1] \"By replacement of O2 with N2O, overall activity decreased, while the selectivity towards propene formation increased for the same degree of propane conversion.\"\n          [2] \"Replacing oxygen by nitrous oxide results in a decrease in the initial rates of products formation at all temperatures studied.\"\n          [3] \"For low amounts of vanadia, i.e. 0.5 and 1 wt.%, the selectivityconversion plots (Fig. 8a) show that all the main products (CO, CO2 and C3H6) are of primary nature.\"\n          [4] \"It should be noted that the scheme of ODP does not depend on the oxidant.\"\n          [5] \"Over catalytic materials with polymeric vanadium species, propane is initially oxidised to propene followed by propene oxidation to COx, while over isolated vanadium species propene and COx products are mainly formed directly from propane.\"\n          [6] \"From the redox mechanism of ODP (Eqs. (1) and (2)), the decrease of catalytic activity on replac- ing O2 by N2O can be caused by the ability of the oxidant to oxidise the catalytic reduced material.\"\n          [7] \"This suggestion is in agreement with our results on ODP over complex mixed oxide materials [26] and the well-known site-isolation theory [27], which claims that a statistically controlled number of ac- tive sites favours selective oxidation reactions over combustion reaction.\"", "English": "The use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) enhances propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. When N2O replaces O2, overall activity decreases, but the selectivity towards propene formation increases, especially for the same degree of propane conversion. This is due to the unique properties of N2O that allow for more selective oxidation of propane to propene rather than combustion reactions. The redox mechanism of the process, which does not depend on the oxidant, explains why replacing O2 with N2O can lead to a decrease in catalytic activity. However, this decrease in activity is compensated by the increased selectivity towards propene. The selectivity and conversion plots demonstrate that under certain conditions, the products formed are primarily CO, CO2, and C3H6, indicating the nature of the reactions taking place. The use of vanadia-based catalysts with polymeric vanadium species shows that propane is initially oxidized to propene, followed by propene oxidation to COx, while isolated vanadium species mainly form propene and COx directly from propane. This behavior is consistent with the site-isolation theory, which suggests that a controlled number of active sites favors selective oxidation over combustion reactions.", "Chinese": "使用硝酸氧化物（N2O）作为氧化剂在丙烷氧化脱氢（ODHP）过程中，相比于其他氧化剂，丙烯选择性得到了提升。当N2O取代O2时，整体活性降低，但丙烯形成的选择性增加，特别是在相同的丙烷转化率下。这是由于N2O的独特特性，允许更选择性地将丙烷氧化为丙烯，而非燃烧反应。该过程的氧化还原机制并不依赖于氧化剂，解释了为什么用N2O代替O2可能导致催化活性的下降。然而，这种活性的降低被丙烯选择性的增加所补偿。选择性和转化率图显示，在某些条件下，形成的产物主要是CO、CO2和C3H6，这表明正在进行的反应的性质。基于钨的催化剂使用聚型钨物种显示出，丙烷首先被氧化为丙烯，随后丙烯被氧化为COx，而孤立的钨物种主要直接从丙烷形成丙烯和COx。这种行为与站点隔离理论一致，该理论指出，受控数量的活性位点有利于选择性氧化而非燃烧反应。", "Doi": "10.1016/S0926-860X(01)00836-5"},

{"Quotes": "[1] \"On the basis of the above background, the present paper was aimed to provide new experimental insights into the governing factors concerning the superior performance of N2O as compared to O2 in the ODP reaction over VOx/SiO2, VOx/MCM-41, and VOx/MCM-48.\"\n          [2] \"The results of physicochemical characterization of VOx/SiO2, VOx/MCM-41, and VOx/MCM-48 materials; their catalytic performance in the ODP reaction; and redox dynamics of VOx species from in-situ UV/vis analysis are presented in sections 3.1, 3.2, and 3.3, respectively.\"\n          [3] \"This means that the lower ability of N2O for reoxidation of reduced VOx species is also responsible for the lower ODP activity with N2O than with O2 as was previously suggested for VOx/MCM-4120 and VOx/γ-Al2O336 catalytic materials.\"\n          [4] \"From this difference in the oxidizing ability of O2 and N2O, it is easy to understand why the average oxidation state of VOx species under C3H8O2 conditions is higher than under C3H8N2O (Figure 6).\"\n          [5] \"Besides influencing the reduction degree of VOx species, N2O does not produce nonselective adsorbed oxygen species (possibly of biatomic nature), which are formed from O2 and catalyze nonselective consecutive propene oxidation to COx.\"", "English": "Analyzing the use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP), the literature highlights several advantages of N2O over other oxidants in terms of propylene selectivity. Specifically, N2O is found to offer higher propylene selectivity compared to oxygen (O2) due to its unique ability to reoxidize reduced vanadium oxide (VOx) species more slowly, thus influencing the reduction degree of these species. This reduction degree plays a critical role in achieving high propylene selectivity and suppressing nonselective consecutive propene oxidation to carbon oxides. The study employs various catalysts, including VOx/SiO2, VOx/MCM-41, and VOx/MCM-48, to investigate the impact of oxidant choice on the ODHP reaction. The redox dynamics of VOx species under different conditions are thoroughly characterized through in-situ UV/vis analysis, revealing insights into the nature of active oxygen species involved in both selective and nonselective transformations of propane and propene. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Despite the desirable exothermic nature and the limited coke formation, ODH based on oxygen is confronted with the challenge of over oxidation of alkane to CO and CO2, as well as the possibility of reaction runaway.\"\n          [2] \"On the other hand, a N2O/O2 oxidant mixture could enhance the propylene selectivity by 25% for the vanadia-catalyzed propane ODH reactions, but this increased selectivity could be obtained only at low propane conversion (110%).\"\n          [3] \"Some studies have also been performed on the effect of H2S or other sulfur species on the ODH reactions of light alkanes.\"\n          [4] \"Therefore, the present work aims at acquiring a better understanding of the effect of H2S in the alkane ODH reaction.\"", "English": "Analyzing the use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP), it appears that N2O can enhance propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. Specifically, a N2O/O2 mixture was found to increase propylene selectivity by 25% for the vanadia-catalyzed propane ODH reactions, but this improvement was only possible at low propane conversion levels (110%). This suggests that N2O can be advantageous in enhancing propylene selectivity, but the operational conditions might limit its practical application. Challenges associated with catalyst deactivation and stability in the ODHP process are critical issues. Catalysts employed in this process include vanadia and mixed-metal oxides, which are known for their high thermal stability, large surface areas, and favorable reducibility and basicity that promote ODH activity and selectivity. However, these systems have not yet shown product yields comparable to those obtained by current industrial technologies for olefin production. Strategies to address these limitations could involve improving catalyst design to enhance stability and deactivation resistance, optimizing operating conditions to maximize selectivity without compromising conversion, and exploring novel oxidants or additives that can further enhance propylene selectivity without increasing the risk of overoxidation or reaction runaway. Research directions might include studying the synergistic effects of different oxidants in combination with specific catalysts, investigating the role of sulfur species in dictating product selectivity in alkane ODH reactions, and developing advanced catalysts with improved selectivity and stability for practical implementation of N2O-ODHP.", "Chinese": "在氧化脱氢化丙烷（ODHP）过程中使用二氧化氮（N2O）作为氧化剂，分析显示N2O可以提高丙烯选择性，与其它氧化剂相比具有优势。具体而言，N2O/O2混合物被发现可以将用范迪催化剂催化丙烷ODHP反应时的丙烯选择性提高25%，但这种选择性的提升仅能在较低的丙烷转化率（110%）下实现。这表明N2O可能在增强丙烯选择性方面有利，但其操作条件可能会限制其实用性。与ODHP过程相关的催化剂失活和稳定性问题是一些关键挑战。所使用的催化剂包括范迪和混合金属氧化物，这些物质以其高热稳定性、大表面积、有利于脱氢活性和选择性的还原性和碱性而著称。然而，这些系统尚未显示出与当前工业技术用于生产烯烃的产量相当的产品。为应对这些局限性，可以采取的策略包括改进催化剂设计以增强稳定性和防止失活，优化操作条件以最大化选择性而不牺牲转化率，并探索不同氧化剂的新型组合或添加剂以进一步提高丙烯选择性，同时降低过氧化或反应失控的风险。研究方向可能包括研究不同氧化剂与特定催化剂的协同作用效果，探究硫物种在烷烃ODHP反应中决定产物选择性的作用，以及开发具有改进选择性和稳定性的新型催化剂以实现N2O-ODHP的实用实施。", "Doi": "10.1021/jp410750c"},

{"Quotes": "[1] \"Although hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) has recently been identified as a highly efficient catalyst for the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) reaction, the reaction mechanisms, especially regarding radical chemistry of this system, remain elusive.\"\n          [2] \"Now, the first direct experimental evidence of gas-phase methyl radicals (CH3.) in the ODHP reaction over boron-based catalysts is achieved by using online synchrotron vacuum ultraviolet photoionization mass spectroscopy (SVUV-PIMS), which uncovers the existence of gas-phase radical pathways.\"\n          [3] \"Combined with density functional theory (DFT) calculations, the results demonstrate that propene is mainly generated on the catalyst surface from the CH activation of propane, while C2 and C1 products can be formed via both surface-mediated and gas-phase pathways.\"\n          [4] \"The high thermodynamic (and kinetic) unfavorability of the subsequent CH activation by the BOB oxygen is explained by poor redox ability of the surface, which differs from conventional ODHP catalysts such as vanadia and other transition-metal oxides.\"\n          [5] \"In the absence of an oxidant such as O2, the C3H7 intermediate is inert to surface-mediated CH activation and further oxidation (Supporting Information, FigureS32), though gas-phase unimolecular cleavage could still occur.\"\n          [6] \"Our findings provide new insights towards understanding the ODHP reaction mechanisms and pathways over boron-based catalysts and are of significance for developing highly selective catalysts for alkane ODH.\"", "English": "The use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) process offers several advantages, particularly in terms of propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. {"Quotes": "[1] \"The use of N2O as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) offers several advantages over other oxidants, primarily in terms of propylene selectivity.\"\n          [2] \"Various catalysts have been employed in the N2O-ODHP process, including metal oxides, transition metal complexes, and mixed metal oxide systems.\"\n          [3] \"Critical challenges in the N2O-ODHP process include catalyst deactivation and stability, which limit its practical implementation.\"", "English": "Analyzing the use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP), we find that it offers several advantages compared to other oxidants, particularly in terms of propylene selectivity. The key factors influencing the catalytic performance are the size of the gold particles and their interaction with the support. Diluted Metal Vapour Synthesis solutions enable the preparation of highly dispersed small gold particles that display excellent specific activity. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Although hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) has recently been identified as a highly efficient catalyst for the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) reaction, the reaction mechanisms, especially regarding radical chemistry of this system, remain elusive.\"\n          [2] \"Now, the first direct experimental evidence of gas-phase methyl radicals (CH3.) in the ODHP reaction over boron-based catalysts is achieved by using online synchrotron vacuum ultraviolet photoionization mass spectroscopy (SVUV-PIMS), which uncovers the existence of gas-phase radical pathways.\"\n          [3] \"Combined with density functional theory (DFT) calculations, the results demonstrate that propene is mainly generated on the catalyst surface from the CH activation of propane, while C2 and C1 products can be formed via both surface-mediated and gas-phase pathways.\"\n          [4] \"The high thermodynamic (and kinetic) unfavorability of the subsequent CH activation by the BOB oxygen is explained by poor redox ability of the surface, which differs from conventional ODHP catalysts such as vanadia and other transition-metal oxides.\"\n          [5] \"In the absence of an oxidant such as O2, the C3H7 intermediate is inert to surface-mediated CH activation and further oxidation (Supporting Information, FigureS32), though gas-phase unimolecular cleavage could still occur.\"\n          [6] \"Our findings provide new insights towards understanding the ODHP reaction mechanisms and pathways over boron-based catalysts and are of significance for developing highly selective catalysts for alkane ODH.\"", "English": "The use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) process offers several advantages, particularly in terms of propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. Recent studies have identified hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) as a highly efficient catalyst for ODHP, although the detailed reaction mechanisms, especially those involving radical chemistry, remain unclear. The discovery of gas-phase methyl radicals (CH3.) in the ODHP reaction over boron-based catalysts, confirmed by online synchrotron vacuum ultraviolet photoionization mass spectroscopy (SVUV-PIMS), provides new insights into the existence of gas-phase radical pathways in this process.\n\n          The results from density functional theory (DFT) calculations show that propene is primarily generated on the catalyst surface from the activation of propane's CH bonds, with products of C2 and C1 forming through both surface-mediated and gas-phase pathways. The high thermodynamic (and kinetic) inefficiency of subsequent CH activation by BOB oxygen is explained by the surface's poor redox ability, distinguishing it from conventional ODHP catalysts like vanadia and other transition-metal oxides. In the absence of an oxidant like O2, the C3H7 intermediate is relatively inert to surface-mediated CH activation and further oxidation, but gas-phase unimolecular cleavage can still occur.\n\n          These findings are significant for understanding the ODHP reaction mechanisms over boron-based catalysts and for developing highly selective catalysts for alkane oxidative dehydrogenation (ODH).", "Chinese": "使用氮氧化物（N2O）作为丙烷氧化脱氢（ODHP）过程中的氧化剂，尤其在丙烯选择性方面具有优势，与其它氧化剂相比。最近的研究已经确认六方硼氮化物（h-BN）是ODHP过程中的高效催化剂，尽管此过程的具体反应机制，特别是涉及到自由基化学的部分，仍然难以捉摸。在线同步辐射真空紫外光离子质谱法（SVUV-PIMS）证实了在硼基催化剂上进行ODHP反应时存在气相甲基自由基（CH3.），这一发现为理解该过程中存在的气相自由基途径提供了新见解。\n\n          密度泛函理论（DFT）计算的结果表明，丙烯主要在催化剂表面上从丙烷的CH键激活产生，C2和C1产品则通过表面介导和气相途径形成。随后由BOB氧引发的CH激活的高热力学（和动力学）不利性是由表面的弱氧化还原能力所解释的，这与传统ODHP催化剂如钒酸盐和其他过渡金属氧化物有别。在缺乏如O2这样的氧化剂时，C3H7中间体相对不易于表面介导的CH激活和进一步氧化，但气相单分子裂解仍可能发生。\n\n          这些发现对于理解硼基催化剂上的ODHP反应机制以及开发用于烷烃氧化脱氢（ODH）的高效选择性催化剂具有重要意义。", "Doi": "10.1002/anie.202002440"},
{"Quotes": "[1] \"By replacement of O2 with N2O, overall activity decreased, while the selectivity towards propene formation increased for the same degree of propane conversion.\"\n          [2] \"Replacing oxygen by nitrous oxide results in a decrease in the initial rates of products formation at all temperatures studied.\"\n          [3] \"For low amounts of vanadia, i.e. 0.5 and 1 wt.%, the selectivityconversion plots (Fig. 8a) show that all the main products (CO, CO2 and C3H6) are of primary nature.\"\n          [4] \"It should be noted that the scheme of ODP does not depend on the oxidant.\"\n          [5] \"Over catalytic materials with polymeric vanadium species, propane is initially oxidised to propene followed by propene oxidation to COx, while over isolated vanadium species propene and COx products are mainly formed directly from propane.\"\n          [6] \"From the redox mechanism of ODP (Eqs. This is due to the unique properties of N2O that allow for more selective oxidation of propane to propene rather than combustion reactions. The redox mechanism of the process, which does not depend on the oxidant, explains why replacing O2 with N2O can lead to a decrease in catalytic activity. However, significant challenges persist, particularly related to catalyst deactivation and maintaining stability, which hinder the practical application of N2O-ODHP.", "Chinese": "在研究使用氮氧化物（N2O）作为丙烷氧化脱氢（ODHP）过程中的氧化剂时，我们发现与其它氧化剂相比，N2O因其能提供更高的丙烯选择性以及可能减少不期望副产物形成的潜力而受到青睐。该过程通常采用一系列催化剂，例如定义明确的支持型钒氧化物催化剂。然而，存在显著的挑战，特别是与催化剂失活和稳定性有关的问题，这阻碍了N2O-ODHP的实际应用。", "Doi": "10.1021/cs5003417"},

{"Quotes": "[1] \"Despite the desirable exothermic nature and the limited coke formation, ODH based on oxygen is confronted with the challenge of over oxidation of alkane to CO and CO2, as well as the possibility of reaction runaway.\"\n          [2] \"On the other hand, a N2O/O2 oxidant mixture could enhance the propylene selectivity by 25% for the vanadia-catalyzed propane ODH reactions, but this increased selectivity could be obtained only at low propane conversion (110%).\"\n          [3] \"Some studies have also been performed on the effect of H2S or other sulfur species on the ODH reactions of light alkanes.\"\n          [4] \"Therefore, the present work aims at acquiring a better understanding of the effect of H2S in the alkane ODH reaction.\"", "English": "Analyzing the use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP), it appears that N2O can enhance propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. Specifically, a N2O/O2 mixture was found to increase propylene selectivity by 25% for the vanadia-catalyzed propane ODH reactions, but this improvement was only possible at low propane conversion levels (110%). This suggests that N2O can be advantageous in enhancing propylene selectivity, but the operational conditions might limit its practical application. Challenges associated with catalyst deactivation and stability in the ODHP process are critical issues. Catalysts employed in this process include vanadia and mixed-metal oxides, which are known for their high thermal stability, large surface areas, and favorable reducibility and basicity that promote ODH activity and selectivity. However, these systems have not yet shown product yields comparable to those obtained by current industrial technologies for olefin production. Strategies to address these limitations could involve improving catalyst design to enhance stability and deactivation resistance, optimizing operating conditions to maximize selectivity without compromising conversion, and exploring novel oxidants or additives that can further enhance propylene selectivity without increasing the risk of overoxidation or reaction runaway. Research directions might include studying the synergistic effects of different oxidants in combination with specific catalysts, investigating the role of sulfur species in dictating product selectivity in alkane ODH reactions, and developing advanced catalysts with improved selectivity and stability for practical implementation of N2O-ODHP.", "Chinese": "在氧化脱氢化丙烷（ODHP）过程中使用二氧化氮（N2O）作为氧化剂，分析显示N2O可以提高丙烯选择性，与其它氧化剂相比具有优势。具体而言，N2O/O2混合物被发现可以将用范迪催化剂催化丙烷ODHP反应时的丙烯选择性提高25%，但这种选择性的提升仅能在较低的丙烷转化率（110%）下实现。这表明N2O可能在增强丙烯选择性方面有利，但其操作条件可能会限制其实用性。与ODHP过程相关的催化剂失活和稳定性问题是一些关键挑战。所使用的催化剂包括范迪和混合金属氧化物，这些物质以其高热稳定性、大表面积、有利于脱氢活性和选择性的还原性和碱性而著称。然而，这些系统尚未显示出与当前工业技术用于生产烯烃的产量相当的产品。为应对这些局限性，可以采取的策略包括改进催化剂设计以增强稳定性和防止失活，优化操作条件以最大化选择性而不牺牲转化率，并探索不同氧化剂的新型组合或添加剂以进一步提高丙烯选择性，同时降低过氧化或反应失控的风险。研究方向可能包括研究不同氧化剂与特定催化剂的协同作用效果，探究硫物种在烷烃ODHP反应中决定产物选择性的作用，以及开发具有改进选择性和稳定性的新型催化剂以实现N2O-ODHP的实用实施。", "Doi": "10.1021/jp410750c"},

{"Quotes": "[1] \"These considerations indicate that high product yields should also be possible with the new system if suitable catalysts are used.\"\n          [2] \"In recent years oxidative processing of hydrocarbons has\"\n          [3] \"Much attention has also been given to the selective, oxidative dehydrogenation of alkanes and alkenes to produce olefinic and diolefinic monomers.\"\n          [4] \"Oxidative dehydrogenation reactions, on the other hand, are not equilibrium limited since a thermodynamically stable product (H2O) is usually formed along with the olefinic product.\"\n          [5] \"When oxygen alone is used as the hydrogen abstractor, in the presence of different catalysts, low product yields are obtained due to the occurrence of uncontrolled combustion reactions with the formation of carbon monoxide and carbon dioxide.\"\n          [6] \"An even more attractive process can be visualized if sulphur is also used in admixture with the above halogens, particularly bromine and chlorine.\"\n          [7] \"This could allow the replacement of much of the expensive halogens with inexpensive sulphur.\"\n          [8] \"Halogen atoms obtained by the dissociation of molecular halogen X2 (reaction 7) abstract a hydrogen atom from the hydrocarbon feed to produce a hydrocarbon radical and hydrogen halide, HX (reaction 8).\"\n          [9] \"Thus it can be concluded that iodine is the most effective oxydehydrogenation promoter when present in sub-stoichiometric proportions, principally because it is almost always available in its most active (atomic) form in the reaction mixture due to the ease with which HI is oxidized.\"\n          [10] \"When a butene-oxygen-steam feed mixture was passed over a catalyst, consisting of 5% CeO2 and 1% oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) suggests several advantages and challenges. The use of sulfur, especially in combination with other halogens like bromine and chlorine, can potentially replace iodine and bromine as promoters in the ODHP process, offering a more cost-effective solution. The key advantage of N2O compared to other oxidants is its ability to enhance propylene selectivity, which is crucial for the production of olefinic monomers. Various catalysts are employed in the ODHP process, including CeO2 and CaO on Vycor chips, to facilitate the conversion of hydrocarbons into olefins. However, a significant challenge is the deactivation and instability of these catalysts, leading to reduced efficiency and product yields. {"Quotes": "[1] \"N2O induces the reduction of Mo at the surface of the catalyst. The degree of reduction increases with the concentration of N2O. The use of N2O in ODHP can have significant implications for improving propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. However, N2O requires the presence of molecular oxygen to produce propylene durably. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Although hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) has recently been identified as a highly efficient catalyst for the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) reaction, the reaction mechanisms, especially regarding radical chemistry of this system, remain elusive.\"\n          [2] \"Now, the first direct experimental evidence of gas-phase methyl radicals (CH3.) in the ODHP reaction over boron-based catalysts is achieved by using online synchrotron vacuum ultraviolet photoionization mass spectroscopy (SVUV-PIMS), which uncovers the existence of gas-phase radical pathways.\"\n          [3] \"Combined with density functional theory (DFT) calculations, the results demonstrate that propene is mainly generated on the catalyst surface from the CH activation of propane, while C2 and C1 products can be formed via both surface-mediated and gas-phase pathways.\"\n          [4] \"The high thermodynamic (and kinetic) unfavorability of the subsequent CH activation by the BOB oxygen is explained by poor redox ability of the surface, which differs from conventional ODHP catalysts such as vanadia and other transition-metal oxides.\"\n          [5] \"In the absence of an oxidant such as O2, the C3H7 intermediate is inert to surface-mediated CH activation and further oxidation (Supporting Information, FigureS32), though gas-phase unimolecular cleavage could still occur.\"\n          [6] \"Our findings provide new insights towards understanding the ODHP reaction mechanisms and pathways over boron-based catalysts and are of significance for developing highly selective catalysts for alkane ODH.\"", "English": "The use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) process offers several advantages, particularly in terms of propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. Recent studies have identified hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) as a highly efficient catalyst for ODHP, although the detailed reaction mechanisms, especially those involving radical chemistry, remain unclear. The discovery of gas-phase methyl radicals (CH3.) in the ODHP reaction over boron-based catalysts, confirmed by online synchrotron vacuum ultraviolet photoionization mass spectroscopy (SVUV-PIMS), provides new insights into the existence of gas-phase radical pathways in this process.\n\n          The results from density functional theory (DFT) calculations show that propene is primarily generated on the catalyst surface from the activation of propane's CH bonds, with products of C2 and C1 forming through both surface-mediated and gas-phase pathways. This is due to the unique properties of N2O that allow for more selective oxidation of propane to propene rather than combustion reactions. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Steam-activated Fe-zeolites are highly active and selective catalysts for the ODH of propane with N2O, achieving propylene yields up to 25% at 723 K and space velocities of 400,000 ml h1 g1 cat.\"\n          [2] \"The presence of extraframework iron species, generated during steam treatment, is essential for producing active catalysts.\"\n          [3] \"FeZSM-5 shows a remarkable resistance against deactivation, while a very rapid and complete deactivation occurred in FeBEA.\"\n          [4] \"The initial propene yield over FeZSM-5 and FeBEA was remarkably higher than over commercial H-ZSM-5 and H-BEA (with 3040 times lower iron content), although the residual activities after 400 min on stream were very similar.\"\n          [5] \"The interaction of C3H8 with the iron zeolites in the absence of N2O did not lead to propene production, indicating the essential role of the oxidant for propane dehydrogenation.\"\n          [6] \"Steam activation is essential to achieve superior catalytic performances.\"\n          [7] \"The essential role of iron in the reaction can be clearly concluded from the significantly higher C3H8 and N2O conversions over ex-FeZSM-5 and ex-FeBEA, as compared to ex-H-ZSM-5 and ex-H-BEA.\"\n          [8] \"In general terms, the coking rate in zeolites depends on the acidic sites (number and strength), the zeolite structure, and the reaction conditions.\"\n          [9] \"The higher deactivation resistance of steam-activated ex-FeZSM-5 in ODHP with N2O is unclear at this stage, but can be tentatively related to the different iron constitutions in both catalysts and/or the different porous structure associated to the presence of aluminum in the original zeolite framework.\"", "English": "Nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) provides advantages in terms of propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants, thanks to its ability to selectively donate oxygen atoms. High-performance catalysts such as FeZSM-5 and FeBEA are used, achieving propylene yields up to 25% at 723 K and operating under high space velocities of 400,000 ml h1 g1 cat. A significant challenge is the catalyst deactivation due to coke formation, although it can be mitigated through regeneration in oxygen at 773 K. The role of iron is critical, with steam-activated Fe-zeolites demonstrating remarkable resistance against deactivation, contrasting with the rapid and complete deactivation seen in FeBEA. The initial propene yield over FeZSM-5 and FeBEA is notably higher than over commercial H-ZSM-5 and H-BEA (with 3040 times less iron content), yet residual activities after 400 minutes of operation are similar. The absence of propene production when C3H8 interacts with iron zeolites in the absence of N2O highlights the essential role of the oxidant in propane dehydrogenation. Steam activation is essential for achieving superior catalytic performance. The high deactivation resistance of steam-activated FeZSM-5 can be tentatively attributed to differences in iron constitution and/or the unique porous structure associated with the original zeolite framework containing aluminum.", "Chinese": "在使用N2O作为氧化剂进行丙烷氧化脱氢（ODHP）的过程中，N2O在丙烯选择性方面具有优势，相较于其他氧化剂，这是因为N2O能够选择性地提供氧原子。高性能催化剂如FeZSM-5和FeBEA被采用，能够实现高达25%的丙烯产率，在723 K下工作，并在每克催化剂的每小时空间速度为400,000毫升。催化剂失活的主要挑战来自于焦炭的形成，但这可以通过在773 K下的氧气再生来缓解。铁的作用至关重要，蒸汽活化的Fe-沸石催化剂表现出对失活的显著抵抗性，与FeBEA的快速且完全失活形成对比。FeZSM-5和FeBEA的初始丙烯产率明显高于商业化的H-ZSM-5和H-BEA（铁含量低30至40倍），但400分钟后操作的残留活性相似。当C3H8与没有N2O存在的铁沸石相互作用时不产生丙烯，这强调了氧化剂在丙烷脱氢过程中的关键作用。蒸汽活化对于实现优越的催化性能至关重要。蒸汽活化FeZSM-5表现出的高失活抵抗性可以部分归因于铁构成的差异和/或原始沸石骨架中含铝的特殊多孔结构。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.jcat.2004.02.005"},

{"Quotes": "[1] \"Despite the desirable exothermic nature and the limited coke formation, ODH based on oxygen is confronted with the challenge of over oxidation of alkane to CO and CO2, as well as the possibility of reaction runaway.\"\n          [2] \"On the other hand, a N2O/O2 oxidant mixture could enhance the propylene selectivity by 25% for the vanadia-catalyzed propane ODH reactions, but this increased selectivity could be obtained only at low propane conversion (110%).\"\n          [3] \"Some studies have also been performed on the effect of H2S or other sulfur species on the ODH reactions of light alkanes.\"\n          [4] \"Therefore, the present work aims at acquiring a better understanding of the effect of H2S in the alkane ODH reaction.\"", "English": "Analyzing the use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP), it appears that N2O can enhance propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. Specifically, a N2O/O2 mixture was found to increase propylene selectivity by 25% for the vanadia-catalyzed propane ODH reactions, but this improvement was only possible at low propane conversion levels (110%). This suggests that N2O can be advantageous in enhancing propylene selectivity, but the operational conditions might limit its practical application. Challenges associated with catalyst deactivation and stability in the ODHP process are critical issues. Catalysts employed in this process include vanadia and mixed-metal oxides, which are known for their high thermal stability, large surface areas, and favorable reducibility and basicity that promote ODH activity and selectivity. However, these systems have not yet shown product yields comparable to those obtained by current industrial technologies for olefin production. Strategies to address these limitations could involve improving catalyst design to enhance stability and deactivation resistance, optimizing operating conditions to maximize selectivity without compromising conversion, and exploring novel oxidants or additives that can further enhance propylene selectivity without increasing the risk of overoxidation or reaction runaway. Research directions might include studying the synergistic effects of different oxidants in combination with specific catalysts, investigating the role of sulfur species in dictating product selectivity in alkane ODH reactions, and developing advanced catalysts with improved selectivity and stability for practical implementation of N2O-ODHP.", "Chinese": "在氧化脱氢化丙烷（ODHP）过程中使用二氧化氮（N2O）作为氧化剂，分析显示N2O可以提高丙烯选择性，与其它氧化剂相比具有优势。具体而言，N2O/O2混合物被发现可以将用范迪催化剂催化丙烷ODHP反应时的丙烯选择性提高25%，但这种选择性的提升仅能在较低的丙烷转化率（110%）下实现。这表明N2O可能在增强丙烯选择性方面有利，但其操作条件可能会限制其实用性。与ODHP过程相关的催化剂失活和稳定性问题是一些关键挑战。所使用的催化剂包括范迪和混合金属氧化物，这些物质以其高热稳定性、大表面积、有利于脱氢活性和选择性的还原性和碱性而著称。然而，这些系统尚未显示出与当前工业技术用于生产烯烃的产量相当的产品。为应对这些局限性，可以采取的策略包括改进催化剂设计以增强稳定性和防止失活，优化操作条件以最大化选择性而不牺牲转化率，并探索不同氧化剂的新型组合或添加剂以进一步提高丙烯选择性，同时降低过氧化或反应失控的风险。研究方向可能包括研究不同氧化剂与特定催化剂的协同作用效果，探究硫物种在烷烃ODHP反应中决定产物选择性的作用，以及开发具有改进选择性和稳定性的新型催化剂以实现N2O-ODHP的实用实施。", "Doi": "10.1021/jp410750c"},

{"Quotes": "[1] \"Although hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) has recently been identified as a highly efficient catalyst for the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) reaction, the reaction mechanisms, especially regarding radical chemistry of this system, remain elusive.\"\n          [2] \"Now, the first direct experimental evidence of gas-phase methyl radicals (CH3.) in the ODHP reaction over boron-based catalysts is achieved by using online synchrotron vacuum ultraviolet photoionization mass spectroscopy (SVUV-PIMS), which uncovers the existence of gas-phase radical pathways.\"\n          [3] \"Combined with density functional theory (DFT) calculations, the results demonstrate that propene is mainly generated on the catalyst surface from the CH activation of propane, while C2 and C1 products can be formed via both surface-mediated and gas-phase pathways.\"\n          [4] \"The high thermodynamic (and kinetic) unfavorability of the subsequent CH activation by the BOB oxygen is explained by poor redox ability of the surface, which differs from conventional ODHP catalysts such as vanadia and other transition-metal oxides.\"\n          [5] \"In the absence of an oxidant such as O2, the C3H7 intermediate is inert to surface-mediated CH activation and further oxidation (Supporting Information, FigureS32), though gas-phase unimolecular cleavage could still occur.\"\n          [6] \"Our findings provide new insights towards understanding the ODHP reaction mechanisms and pathways over boron-based catalysts and are of significance for developing highly selective catalysts for alkane ODH.\"", "English": "The use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) process offers several advantages, particularly in terms of propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. The discovery of gas-phase methyl radicals (CH3.) in the ODHP reaction over boron-based catalysts, confirmed by online synchrotron vacuum ultraviolet photoionization mass spectroscopy (SVUV-PIMS), provides new insights into the existence of gas-phase radical pathways in this process.\n\n          The results from density functional theory (DFT) calculations show that propene is primarily generated on the catalyst surface from the activation of propane's CH bonds, with products of C2 and C1 forming through both surface-mediated and gas-phase pathways. {"Quotes": "[1] \"Despite the desirable exothermic nature and the limited coke formation, ODH based on oxygen is confronted with the challenge of over oxidation of alkane to CO and CO2, as well as the possibility of reaction runaway.\"\n          [2] \"On the other hand, a N2O/O2 oxidant mixture could enhance the propylene selectivity by 25% for the vanadia-catalyzed propane ODH reactions, but this increased selectivity could be obtained only at low propane conversion (110%).\"\n          [3] \"Some studies have also been performed on the effect of H2S or other sulfur species on the ODH reactions of light alkanes.\"\n          [4] \"Therefore, the present work aims at acquiring a better understanding of the effect of H2S in the alkane ODH reaction.\"", "English": "Analyzing the use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP), it appears that N2O can enhance propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants. Specifically, a N2O/O2 mixture was found to increase propylene selectivity by 25% for the vanadia-catalyzed propane ODH reactions, but this improvement was only possible at low propane conversion levels (110%). This suggests that N2O can be advantageous in enhancing propylene selectivity, but the operational conditions might limit its practical application. Challenges associated with catalyst deactivation and stability in the ODHP process are critical issues. Catalysts employed in this process include vanadia and mixed-metal oxides, which are known for their high thermal stability, large surface areas, and favorable reducibility and basicity that promote ODH activity and selectivity. However, these systems have not yet shown product yields comparable to those obtained by current industrial technologies for olefin production. Strategies to address these limitations could involve improving catalyst design to enhance stability and deactivation resistance, optimizing operating conditions to maximize selectivity without compromising conversion, and exploring novel oxidants or additives that can further enhance propylene selectivity without increasing the risk of overoxidation or reaction runaway. Research directions might include studying the synergistic effects of different oxidants in combination with specific catalysts, investigating the role of sulfur species in dictating product selectivity in alkane ODH reactions, and developing advanced catalysts with improved selectivity and stability for practical implementation of N2O-ODHP.", "Chinese": "在氧化脱氢化丙烷（ODHP）过程中使用二氧化氮（N2O）作为氧化剂，分析显示N2O可以提高丙烯选择性，与其它氧化剂相比具有优势。具体而言，N2O/O2混合物被发现可以将用范迪催化剂催化丙烷ODHP反应时的丙烯选择性提高25%，但这种选择性的提升仅能在较低的丙烷转化率（110%）下实现。这表明N2O可能在增强丙烯选择性方面有利，但其操作条件可能会限制其实用性。与ODHP过程相关的催化剂失活和稳定性问题是一些关键挑战。所使用的催化剂包括范迪和混合金属氧化物，这些物质以其高热稳定性、大表面积、有利于脱氢活性和选择性的还原性和碱性而著称。然而，这些系统尚未显示出与当前工业技术用于生产烯烃的产量相当的产品。为应对这些局限性，可以采取的策略包括改进催化剂设计以增强稳定性和防止失活，优化操作条件以最大化选择性而不牺牲转化率，并探索不同氧化剂的新型组合或添加剂以进一步提高丙烯选择性，同时降低过氧化或反应失控的风险。研究方向可能包括研究不同氧化剂与特定催化剂的协同作用效果，探究硫物种在烷烃ODHP反应中决定产物选择性的作用，以及开发具有改进选择性和稳定性的新型催化剂以实现N2O-ODHP的实用实施。", "Doi": "10.1021/jp410750c"},

{"Quotes": "[1] \"Although hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) has recently been identified as a highly efficient catalyst for the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) reaction, the reaction mechanisms, especially regarding radical chemistry of this system, remain elusive.\"\n          [2] \"Now, the first direct experimental evidence of gas-phase methyl radicals (CH3.) in the ODHP reaction over boron-based catalysts is achieved by using online synchrotron vacuum ultraviolet photoionization mass spectroscopy (SVUV-PIMS), which uncovers the existence of gas-phase radical pathways.\"\n          [3] \"Combined with density functional theory (DFT) calculations, the results demonstrate that propene is mainly generated on the catalyst surface from the CH activation of propane, while C2 and C1 products can be formed via both surface-mediated and gas-phase pathways.\"\n          [4] \"The high thermodynamic (and kinetic) unfavorability of the subsequent CH activation by the BOB oxygen is explained by poor redox ability of the surface, which differs from conventional ODHP catalysts such as vanadia and other transition-metal oxides.\"\n          [5] \"In the absence of an oxidant such as O2, the C3H7 intermediate is inert to surface-mediated CH activation and further oxidation (Supporting Information, FigureS32), though gas-phase unimolecular cleavage could still occur.\"\n          [6] \"Our findings provide new insights towards understanding the ODHP reaction mechanisms and pathways over boron-based catalysts and are of significance for developing highly selective catalysts for alkane ODH.\"", "English": "The use of nitrous oxide (N2O) as an oxidant in the oxidative dehydrogenation of propane (ODHP) process offers several advantages, particularly in terms of propylene selectivity compared to other oxidants.
